= –Ф–Њ—Б—В—Г–њ–љ–Њ –њ–Њ—Б–ї–µ –±–∞–Ј—Л
${money(model.freeCash)}

${money(model.recommendedDebtPayment)}

`; } function expenseShareBars(p){ const ex=state.operations.filter(o=>o.type==='expense'&&inPeriod(o.date,p)); if(!ex.length) return empty('–†–∞—Б—Е–Њ–і–Њ–≤ –њ–Њ–Ї–∞ –љ–µ—В'); const m={}; ex.forEach(o=>m[o.category||'–С–µ–Ј –Ї–∞—В–µ–≥–Њ—А–Є–Є']=(m[o.category||'–С–µ–Ј –Ї–∞—В–µ–≥–Њ—А–Є–Є']||0)+num(o.amount)); const rows=Object.entries(m).sort((a,b)=>b[1]-a[1]); const max=rows[0][1]||1; return `
${rows.slice(0,6).map(([k,v])=>`
${esc(k)}
${money(v)}
`).join('')}
`; } function financeGoalsBlock(){ const goals=financialGoalsOnly(); return `

–§–Є–љ–∞–љ—Б–Њ–≤—Л–µ —Ж–µ–ї–Є –Є –љ–∞–Ї–Њ–њ–ї–µ–љ–Є—П

–І—В–Њ–±—Л –љ–µ —В–Њ–ї—М–Ї–Њ –Ј–∞–Ї—А—Л–≤–∞—В—М –і–Њ–ї–≥–Є, –љ–Њ –Є —Б—В—А–Њ–Є—В—М –Ј–∞–њ–∞—Б –Є –±–Њ–ї—М—И–Є–µ —Б—Г–Љ–Љ—Л.

${goals.length?`
${goals.map(g=>{const p=g.target?clamp(Math.round(num(g.current)/Math.max(1,num(g.target))*100)):0;return `

${esc(g.title)}

${esc(g.area||'–§–Є–љ–∞–љ—Б—Л')} ¬Ј —Б—А–Њ–Ї ${fmt(g.deadline)}

${p}%
${prog(p,'green')}
–°–µ–є—З–∞—Б${money(g.current)}
–¶–µ–ї—М${money(g.target)}
–®–∞–≥ –љ–µ–і–µ–ї–Є${esc((g.note||'–Ю–і–Є–љ –Ї–Њ–љ–Ї—А–µ—В–љ—Л–є —И–∞–≥ –љ–∞ –љ–µ–і–µ–ї—О').slice(0,60))}
`}).join('')}
`:`
–Ф–Њ–±–∞–≤—М —Е–Њ—В—П –±—Л 2 —Д–Є–љ–∞–љ—Б–Њ–≤—Л–µ —Ж–µ–ї–Є: –њ–Њ–і—Г—И–Ї–∞ –±–µ–Ј–Њ–њ–∞—Б–љ–Њ—Б—В–Є –Є —Б—Г–Љ–Љ–∞ –і–ї—П –љ–∞–Ї–Њ–њ–ї–µ–љ–Є—П. –Ґ–∞–Ї –њ—А–Є–ї–Њ–ґ–µ–љ–Є–µ –±—Г–і–µ—В –њ–Њ–Ї–∞–Ј—Л–≤–∞—В—М –љ–µ —В–Њ–ї—М–Ї–Њ –і–Њ–ї–≥–Є, –љ–Њ –Є —В–≤–Њ–є –њ—А–Њ–≥—А–µ—Б—Б –Ї —Д–Є–љ–∞–љ—Б–Њ–≤–Њ–є —Б–≤–Њ–±–Њ–і–µ.
`}
`; } function debtRepayPlan(out){ return debtPayoffOrder(out).map((d,i)=>{ const dd=d.due?daysBetween(today(),d.due):null; const tone = d.due && d.due${rows.map(r=>`
${r.index}

${esc(r.debt.person)}

${r.note}

${money(r.debt.amount)}
${esc(r.debt.note||'–С–µ–Ј –Ї–Њ–Љ–Љ–µ–љ—В–∞—А–Є—П')}
`).join('')}
`:empty('–Э–µ—В –∞–Ї—В–Є–≤–љ—Л—Е –і–Њ–ї–≥–Њ–≤'); } function dueTimeline(list, title, emptyText){ return `

${title}

${list.length?list.map(d=>`
${esc(d.person)}
${d.direction==='out'?'–ѓ –і–Њ–ї–ґ–µ–љ':'–Ь–љ–µ –і–Њ–ї–ґ–љ—Л'} ¬Ј ${fmt(d.due)}
${money(d.amount)}
${esc(d.note||'–С–µ–Ј –Ї–Њ–Љ–Љ–µ–љ—В–∞—А–Є—П')}
`).join(''):`
${emptyText}
`}
`; } financePage = function(){ ensureFinanceDebtV27Styles(); const p=periodInfo(); const model=financeModel(p); const nextDebt = debtPayoffOrder(model.out)[0]; return layout('–§–Є–љ–∞–љ—Б—Л','–Ф–µ–љ—М–≥–Є –њ–Њ–і –Ї–Њ–љ—В—А–Њ–ї–µ–Љ: —Б–љ–∞—З–∞–ї–∞ –њ–Њ—А—П–і–Њ–Ї, –Ј–∞—В–µ–Љ –Ј–∞–Ї—А—Л—В–Є–µ –і–Њ–ї–≥–Њ–≤ –Є –љ–∞–Ї–Њ–њ–ї–µ–љ–Є–µ —Б—Г–Љ–Љ.',`
${[['month','–Ґ–µ–Ї—Г—Й–Є–є –Љ–µ—Б—П—Ж'],['last','–Я—А–Њ—И–ї—Л–є'],['next','–С—Г–і—Г—Й–Є–є –Љ–µ—Б—П—Ж'],['quarter','3 –Љ–µ—Б—П—Ж–∞'],['year','–У–Њ–і']].map(([k,l])=>``).join('')}

${money(state.settings.currentBalance)}

${money(model.t.inc)}
–Т—Б–µ –і–Њ—Е–Њ–і—Л –Ј–∞ –≤—Л–±—А–∞–љ–љ—Л–є –њ–µ—А–Є–Њ–і.

${money(Math.max(3000,Math.round((state.settings.currentBalance||0)*0.15/1000)*1000))}

${money(potentialNet)}

, TAB, –і–∞—В—Л 2026-07-07 / 07.07.2026, –Ї–Њ–і–Є—А–Њ–≤–Ї–∞ UTF-8 –Є–ї–Є Windows-1251. –Ф—Г–±–ї–Є –њ—А–Њ–њ—Г—Б–Ї–∞—О—В—Б—П –∞–≤—В–Њ–Љ–∞—В–Є—З–µ—Б–Ї–Є.'; box.appendChild(hint); } }); const v=document.querySelector('.version'); } function v39SetStatus(el,msg){ const box=v39ClosestCsvBox(el); const s=box.querySelector?.('.v39-csv-status'); if(s) s.textContent=msg; } async function v39ReadText(file){ const buf=await file.arrayBuffer(); } function v39DetectDelimiter(lines){ const sample=lines.slice(0,12).join('\n'); const opts=[';',',','\t']; let best=';', score=-1; opts.forEach(d=>{ let count=0, q=false; for(let i=0;iscore){score=count;best=d;} }); return best; } function v39ParseLine(line,delim){ const out=[]; let cur='', q=false; for(let i=0;iString(x||'').trim().replace(/^"|"$/g,'')); } function v39ParseRows(text){ const lines=String(text||'').replace(/\r\n/g,'\n').replace(/\r/g,'\n').split('\n').map(x=>x.trim()).filter(Boolean); if(!lines.length) return []; const delim=v39DetectDelimiter(lines); return lines.map(line=>v39ParseLine(line,delim)).filter(r=>r.some(Boolean)); } function v39NormHeader(s){return String(s||'').toLowerCase().replace(/[—С]/g,'–µ').replace(/\s+/g,' ').trim();} function v39FindHeaderIndex(headers,words){ return headers.findIndex(h=>words.some(w=>h.includes(w))); } function v39Money(v){ let s=String(v??'').replace(/\u00a0/g,' ').trim(); if(!s) return 0; let neg=/^\(.*\)$/.test(s) || /^-/.test(s) || /—А–∞—Б—Е–Њ–і|—Б–њ–Є—Б–∞–љ|debit|withdraw/i.test(s); s=s.replace(/[()вВљ—А—А—Г–±RUBrub]/g,'').replace(/\s/g,'').replace(/[+]/g,''); if((s.match(/,/g)||[]).length===1 && (s.match(/\./g)||[]).length===0) s=s.replace(',','.'); else if(s.includes(',')&&s.includes('.')){ if(s.lastIndexOf(',')>s.lastIndexOf('.')) s=s.replace(/\./g,'').replace(',','.'); else s=s.replace(/,/g,''); } const n=parseFloat(s.replace(/[^0-9.\-]/g,'')); if(!Number.isFinite(n)) return 0; return neg?-Math.abs(n):n; } function v39Date(v){ const s=String(v||'').trim(); let m=s.match(/(20\d{2})[-/.](\d{1,2})[-/.](\d{1,2})/); if(m) return `${m[1]}-${m[2].padStart(2,'0')}-${m[3].padStart(2,'0')}`; m=s.match(/(\d{1,2})[-/.](\d{1,2})[-/.](20\d{2})/); if(m) return `${m[3]}-${m[2].padStart(2,'0')}-${m[1].padStart(2,'0')}`; return today(); } function v39LooksHeader(row){ const s=row.map(v39NormHeader).join(' | '); return /–і–∞—В–∞|date|—Б—Г–Љ–Љ–∞|amount|–Њ–њ–Є—Б–∞–љ–Є–µ|–љ–∞–Ј–љ–∞—З–µ–љ–Є–µ|–Њ–њ–µ—А–∞—Ж|–њ—А–Є—Е–Њ–і|—А–∞—Б—Е–Њ–і|debit|credit/.test(s) && !/\d{1,2}[./-]\d{1,2}[./-]20\d{2}/.test(s); } function v39GuessCategory(note,type){ const s=String(note||'').toLowerCase(); if(type==='income') return '–Ф–Њ—Е–Њ–і'; if(/–њ—А–Њ–і—Г–Ї—В|–Љ–∞–≥–љ–Є—В|–њ—П—В–µ—А|–њ–µ—А–µ–Ї—А–µ—Б—В|–ї–∞–≤–Ї–∞|market|ozon|wildberries|wb/i.test(s)) return '–Я—А–Њ–і—Г–Ї—В—Л / –њ–Њ–Ї—Г–њ–Ї–Є'; return '–С–∞–љ–Ї'; } function v39RowsToOps(rows){ if(!rows.length) return []; let header=null, data=rows; if(v39LooksHeader(rows[0])){ header=rows[0].map(v39NormHeader); data=rows.slice(1); } let idx={}; } const ops=[]; data.forEach(row=>{ if(!row || row.length<2) return; let date=today(), amount=0, type='', category='', note=''; if(header){ date=v39Date(row[idx.date]||row[0]); const debit=idx.debit>=0?v39Money(row[idx.debit]):0; const credit=idx.credit>=0?v39Money(row[idx.credit]):0; if(debit){amount=Math.abs(debit);type='expense';} if(credit){amount=Math.abs(credit);type='income';} if(!amount && idx.amount>=0){amount=v39Money(row[idx.amount]);type=amount<0?'expense':'income';amount=Math.abs(amount);} const t=idx.type>=0?v39NormHeader(row[idx.type]):''; amount=v39Money(amountCell); type=amount<0?'expense':'income'; amount=Math.abs(amount); note=row.filter(x=>x!==dateCell&&x!==amountCell).slice(0,4).join(' ¬Ј ')||'–Ш–Љ–њ–Њ—А—В –±–∞–љ–Ї–∞'; } if(!amount) return; `; document.head.appendChild(st); } function v40DaysLeft(p){return Math.max(1, Math.ceil((new Date(p.end)-new Date(today()))/86400000)+1)} function v40Ops(p){return state.operations.filter(o=>inPeriod(o.date,p))} function v40Expenses(p){return v40Ops(p).filter(o=>o.type==='expense')} function v40Income(p){return v40Ops(p).filter(o=>o.type==='income')} function v40OutDebts(){return activeDebts().filter(d=>d.direction==='out')} function v40InDebts(){return activeDebts().filter(d=>d.direction==='in')} function v40DueDays(d){return d.due?Math.ceil((new Date(d.due)-new Date(today()))/86400000):9999} function v40DebtPriority(){return v40OutDebts().slice().sort((a,b)=>{const ao=a.due&&a.dueo.type===type).forEach(o=>{m[o.category||'–С–µ–Ј –Ї–∞—В–µ–≥–Њ—А–Є–Є']=(m[o.category||'–С–µ–Ј –Ї–∞—В–µ–≥–Њ—А–Є–Є']||0)+num(o.amount)});return m} function v40TopCategory(p){const rows=Object.entries(v40CategoryMap(p,'expense')).sort((a,b)=>b[1]-a[1]);return rows[0]||['–Э–µ—В —А–∞—Б—Е–Њ–і–Њ–≤',0]} function v40DailyStats(p,t){const days=Math.max(1,Math.ceil((new Date(p.end)-new Date(p.start))/86400000)+1);const passed=Math.max(1,Math.ceil((new Date(today())-new Date(p.start))/86400000)+1);const daysLeft=v40DaysLeft(p);const spent=t.exp;const avg=spent/Math.max(1,passed);const projected=avg*days;return{days,passed,daysLeft,avg,projected}} function v40Model(){const p=periodInfo();const t=financeTotals(p);const out=v40OutDebts();const incDebts=v40InDebts();const overdue=out.filter(d=>d.due&&d.duev40DueDays(d)>=0&&v40DueDays(d)<=7);const next=v40DebtPriority()[0];const stats=v40DailyStats(p,t);const baseLeft=state.settings.currentBalance+t.inc-t.exp-t.upcoming;const mandatory=total(overdue)+total(due7);const reserve=Math.max(0,Math.min(baseLeft-mandatory, Math.round(Math.max(0,baseLeft-mandatory)*0.2/500)*500));const debtPay=Math.max(0,Math.round(Math.max(mandatory, Math.max(0,baseLeft-reserve)*0.65)/500)*500);const free=Math.max(0,baseLeft-debtPay-reserve);const dayLimit=Math.max(0, Math.round(free/Math.max(1,stats.daysLeft)/100)*100);const scoreParts=[t.inc>0?25:5, t.exp<=t.inc?20:5, baseLeft>=0?20:5, overdue.length?0:15, reserve>0?10:2, dayLimit>0?10:2];const score=clamp(scoreParts.reduce((a,b)=>a+b,0),0,100);const top=v40TopCategory(p);return{p,t,out,incDebts,overdue,due7,next,stats,baseLeft,mandatory,reserve,debtPay,free,dayLimit,score,top};} function v40Tone(n){return n<0?'red':n>0?'green':'blue'} function v40StatusText(m){if(m.score>=80)return ['–§–Є–љ–∞–љ—Б–Њ–≤–Њ —Б–њ–Њ–Ї–Њ–є–љ–Њ','green','–°–Є—Б—В–µ–Љ–∞ –≤ –њ–Њ—А—П–і–Ї–µ: –і–µ–љ—М–≥–Є, –і–Њ–ї–≥–Є –Є —А–µ–Ј–µ—А–≤ –њ–Њ–і –Ї–Њ–љ—В—А–Њ–ї–µ–Љ.'];if(m.score>=55)return ['–Э—Г–ґ–µ–љ –Ї–Њ–љ—В—А–Њ–ї—М','amber','–Х—Б—В—М —А–∞–±–Њ—З–Є–є –Ј–∞–њ–∞—Б, –љ–Њ –≤–∞–ґ–љ–Њ –љ–µ –њ–µ—А–µ–≥—А—Г–Ј–Є—В—М –Љ–µ—Б—П—Ж –њ–Њ–Ї—Г–њ–Ї–∞–Љ–Є –Є –і–Њ–ї–≥–∞–Љ–Є.'];return ['–Ч–Њ–љ–∞ —А–Є—Б–Ї–∞','red','–Э—Г–ґ–µ–љ —А–µ–ґ–Є–Љ –Ј–∞—Й–Є—В—Л: —В–Њ–ї—М–Ї–Њ –Њ–±—П–Ј–∞—В–µ–ї—М–љ—Л–µ —В—А–∞—В—Л, –і–Њ–ї–≥–Є –њ–Њ —Б—А–Њ–Ї–∞–Љ –Є –Љ–Є–љ–Є–Љ—Г–Љ –≤ —А–µ–Ј–µ—А–≤.'];} function v40MainRisk(m){if(m.overdue.length)return `–Я—А–Њ—Б—А–Њ—З–µ–љ–Њ ${money(total(m.overdue))}. –°–љ–∞—З–∞–ї–∞ –Ј–∞–Ї—А—Л—В—М –Є–ї–Є –і–Њ–≥–Њ–≤–Њ—А–Є—В—М—Б—П –њ–Њ —Б—А–Њ–Ї–∞–Љ.`;if(m.due7.length)return `–Т –±–ї–Є–ґ–∞–є—И–Є–µ 7 –і–љ–µ–є –Ї –Њ–њ–ї–∞—В–µ ${money(total(m.due7))}. –Э–µ –њ–ї–∞–љ–Є—А–Њ–≤–∞—В—М –ї–Є—И–љ–Є–µ –њ–Њ–Ї—Г–њ–Ї–Є.`;if(m.t.upcoming>m.free)return `–Я–ї–∞–љ–Њ–≤—Л–µ –њ–Њ–Ї—Г–њ–Ї–Є ${money(m.t.upcoming)} –і–∞–≤—П—В –љ–∞ –Њ—Б—В–∞—В–Њ–Ї. –І–∞—Б—В—М –ї—Г—З—И–µ –њ–µ—А–µ–љ–µ—Б—В–Є.`;if(m.stats.projected>m.t.inc&&m.t.inc>0)return '–Ґ–µ–Љ–њ —А–∞—Б—Е–Њ–і–Њ–≤ –≤—Л—И–µ –і–Њ—Е–Њ–і–∞. –Э—Г–ґ–µ–љ –і–љ–µ–≤–љ–Њ–є –ї–Є–Љ–Є—В.';return '–Ъ—А–Є—В–Є—З–µ—Б–Ї–Є—Е —А–Є—Б–Ї–Њ–≤ –љ–µ –≤–Є–і–љ–Њ. –У–ї–∞–≤–љ–Њ–µ вАФ –љ–µ —Г–≤–µ–ї–Є—З–Є–≤–∞—В—М –і–Њ–ї–≥–Њ–≤—Г—О –љ–∞–≥—А—Г–Ј–Ї—Г.';} function v40MainAction(m){if(m.next)return `–Я—А–Є–Њ—А–Є—В–µ—В –і–Њ–ї–≥–∞: ${esc(m.next.person)} ¬Ј ${money(m.next.amount)} ¬Ј ${m.next.due?fmt(m.next.due):'–±–µ–Ј —Б—А–Њ–Ї–∞'}.`;if(m.reserve>0)return `–Ю—В–ї–Њ–ґ–Є—В—М ${money(m.reserve)} –≤ —А–µ–Ј–µ—А–≤ –і–Њ –ї—О–±—Л—Е –љ–µ–Њ–±—П–Ј–∞—В–µ–ї—М–љ—Л—Е —В—А–∞—В.`;return `–Ф–µ—А–ґ–∞—В—М –і–љ–µ–≤–љ–Њ–є –ї–Є–Љ–Є—В ${money(m.dayLimit)} –Є –љ–µ –±—А–∞—В—М –љ–Њ–≤—Л–µ –Њ–±—П–Ј–∞—В–µ–ї—М—Б—В–≤–∞.`;} function v40Kpi(label,numText,sub,cls='blue'){return `
${label}
${numText}
${sub}

`;} function v40ActionList(m){const items=[];items.push(`–Ф–µ—А–ґ–∞—В—М –і–љ–µ–≤–љ–Њ–є –ї–Є–Љ–Є—В ${money(m.dayLimit)} –і–Њ –Ї–Њ–љ—Ж–∞ –њ–µ—А–Є–Њ–і–∞.`);if(m.next)items.push(`–Ч–∞–Ї—А—Л—В—М / —З–∞—Б—В–Є—З–љ–Њ –Ј–∞–Ї—А—Л—В—М: ${esc(m.next.person)} –љ–∞ ${money(Math.min(num(m.next.amount),Math.max(0,m.debtPay)))}.`);if(m.reserve>0)items.push(`–°—А–∞–Ј—Г –Њ—В–ї–Њ–ґ–Є—В—М ${money(m.reserve)} –≤ —А–µ–Ј–µ—А–≤.`);if(m.t.upcoming>0)items.push(`–Я—А–Њ–≤–µ—А–Є—В—М –њ–ї–∞–љ–Њ–≤—Л–µ –њ–Њ–Ї—Г–њ–Ї–Є –љ–∞ ${money(m.t.upcoming)} –Є —Г–±—А–∞—В—М –љ–µ–Њ–±—П–Ј–∞—В–µ–ї—М–љ—Л–µ.`);items.push(`–Ш–Љ–њ–Њ—А—В–Є—А–Њ–≤–∞—В—М –Њ–њ–µ—А–∞—Ж–Є–Є –Р–ї—М—Д–∞-–С–∞–љ–Ї–∞ –Є–ї–Є CSV, —З—В–Њ–±—Л –∞–љ–∞–ї–Є—В–Є–Ї–∞ –±—Л–ї–∞ —В–Њ—З–љ–Њ–є.`);return `

`} function v40Insights(m){const cat=m.top;const ops=v40Ops(m.p);const expOps=v40Expenses(m.p);const small=expOps.filter(o=>num(o.amount)<1000).length;const big=expOps.slice().sort((a,b)=>num(b.amount)-num(a.amount))[0];const purchasePressure=m.t.inc?Math.round(m.t.upcoming/Math.max(1,m.t.inc)*100):0;const pace=m.stats.projected-m.t.exp;const rows=[['–У–ї–∞–≤–љ–∞—П –Ї–∞—В–µ–≥–Њ—А–Є—П',`${cat[0]} ¬Ј ${money(cat[1])}`,`–°–∞–Љ–∞—П –±–Њ–ї—М—И–∞—П —Б—В–∞—В—М—П —А–∞—Б—Е–Њ–і–Њ–≤ –Ј–∞ –њ–µ—А–Є–Њ–і.`],['–Ґ–µ–Љ–њ —В—А–∞—В',`${money(m.stats.avg)} / –і–µ–љ—М`,`–Х—Б–ї–Є —В–µ–Љ–њ —Б–Њ—Е—А–∞–љ–Є—В—Б—П, —А–∞—Б—Е–Њ–і—Л –±—Г–і—Г—В –Њ–Ї–Њ–ї–Њ ${money(m.stats.projected)}.`],['–Ь–µ–ї–Ї–Є–µ —В—А–∞—В—Л',`${small} –Њ–њ–µ—А–∞—Ж–Є–є –і–Њ 1 000 вВљ`,`–Ш—Е –ї—Г—З—И–µ —Б–Љ–Њ—В—А–µ—В—М –њ–∞—З–Ї–Њ–є: –Є–Љ–µ–љ–љ–Њ –Њ–љ–Є —З–∞—Б—В–Њ –љ–µ–Ј–∞–Љ–µ—В–љ–Њ —Б—К–µ–і–∞—О—В –Њ—Б—В–∞—В–Њ–Ї.`],['–Ъ—А—Г–њ–љ–∞—П —В—А–∞—В–∞',big?`${money(big.amount)} ¬Ј ${esc(big.category||'')}`:'–Э–µ—В –Ї—А—Г–њ–љ—Л—Е —В—А–∞—В',big?esc((big.note||'–С–µ–Ј –Ї–Њ–Љ–Љ–µ–љ—В–∞—А–Є—П').slice(0,90)):'–Ч–∞ –њ–µ—А–Є–Њ–і –Ї—А—Г–њ–љ—Л—Е —А–∞—Б—Е–Њ–і–Њ–≤ –љ–µ –љ–∞–є–і–µ–љ–Њ.'],['–Я–Њ–Ї—Г–њ–Ї–Є –±—Г–і—Г—Й–Є—Е –і–љ–µ–є',`${money(m.t.upcoming)} ¬Ј ${purchasePressure}% –і–Њ—Е–Њ–і–∞`,`–Я–ї–∞–љ–Њ–≤—Л–µ –њ–Њ–Ї—Г–њ–Ї–Є –Ј–∞—А–∞–љ–µ–µ —Г—З–Є—В—Л–≤–∞—О—В—Б—П –≤ –њ—А–Њ–≥–љ–Њ–Ј–µ.`],['–Ю–њ–µ—А–∞—Ж–Є–є –≤ –њ–µ—А–Є–Њ–і–µ',`${ops.length}`,`–І–µ–Љ —З–∞—Й–µ –Њ–±–љ–Њ–≤–ї—П–µ—И—М –і–∞–љ–љ—Л–µ –±–∞–љ–Ї–∞, —В–µ–Љ —В–Њ—З–љ–µ–µ —А–µ–Ї–Њ–Љ–µ–љ–і–∞—Ж–Є–Є.`]];return `
${rows.map(r=>`
